if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_14();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'c360452efd24eb3a78e7bfecbd81fc9576abb3f9') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'c360452efd24eb3a78e7bfecbd81fc9576abb3f9') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '6c168fce82b509bb64441813ca491edae8f364d3') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_14();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'c360452efd24eb3a78e7bfecbd81fc9576abb3f9') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
	writefile_15();
	if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt') != 'd6e9c82f6b4fcdcc7e74d6a8e6005a5ee90e570e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt') !== 'd6e9c82f6b4fcdcc7e74d6a8e6005a5ee90e570e') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt') !== '2990080418a77613546958edc47dfa0e492189df') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_15();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt') !== 'd6e9c82f6b4fcdcc7e74d6a8e6005a5ee90e570e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/oidplus_functions.js');
	writefile_17();
	if (!is_file('includes/oidplus_functions.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oidplus_functions.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oidplus_functions.js') != '0368f1566508dded4ed9ce13aed4fdb1f4d2f321') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_functions.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oidplus_functions.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oidplus_functions.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_functions.js') !== '0368f1566508dded4ed9ce13aed4fdb1f4d2f321') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_functions.js') !== 'cc6b137f4a70d8e37c96816b219279e3ca4af986') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oidplus_functions.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oidplus_functions.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oidplus_functions.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oidplus_functions.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_functions.js') !== '0368f1566508dded4ed9ce13aed4fdb1f4d2f321') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_functions.js');
		}
	}

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/820_login_facebook/OIDplusPagePublicLoginFacebook.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/820_login_facebook/OIDplusPagePublicLoginFacebook.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_28();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/820_login_facebook/OIDplusPagePublicLoginFacebook.class.php') !== 'b94fcdc1b281a4c6b08fc5d32ff90a0f69b469ad') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/820_login_facebook/OIDplusPagePublicLoginFacebook.class.php');
		}
	}
}

// File deleted: plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/125_forgot_password_admin/OIDplusPagePublicForgotPasswordAdmin2.class.php
@unlink('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/125_forgot_password_admin/OIDplusPagePublicForgotPasswordAdmin2.class.php');
if (is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/125_forgot_password_admin/OIDplusPagePublicForgotPasswordAdmin2.class.php')) {
	warn('File could not be deleted: plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/125_forgot_password_admin/OIDplusPagePublicForgotPasswordAdmin2.class.php');
}


file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 1000\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 1000') err('Could not write to .version.php!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
